+# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# I-deepfix-006 A/B (#1376) — INLINE furniture strip (SPAN-LEVEL, suppress-only, source NEVER deleted).
+#
+# THE GAP (Fable A/B root cause): the furniture predicates above route a WHOLE unit to the ledger or
+# drop it, but a fixed boilerplate FRAGMENT welded INSIDE an otherwise-real clause survives — e.g.
+# "An official website of the United States government The unemployment rate fell 0.4%", a "Crossref 0"
+# citation-count widget glued to a finding, a "5 Minute Read Time" reader token, a "02-10-2025" date
+# stamp, or IMF working-paper front-matter ("© 2025 International Monetary Fund", "WP/25/123",
+# "Prepared by …", "Authorized for distribution by …", "The authors would like to thank …") lifted into
+# the same extraction blob as a real sentence. This EXCISES the boilerplate fragment while KEEPING the
+# surrounding clause. It never touches the evidence pool, the bibliography, or a faithfulness verdict —
+# removing furniture text can only SHORTEN a rendered unit, never fabricate a number/word (all numeric
+# comparison stays with the frozen strict_verify). §-1.3.1 span-level carve-out.
+#
+# FAITHFULNESS SAFETY: fixed-token furniture (gov banner / Crossref widget / reading-time / WP number /
+# date stamp) never carries a finding, so it is excised unconditionally. The clause-form front-matter
+# (IMF copyright / "Prepared by" / "Authorized for distribution by" / acknowledgements) is excised ONLY
+# when the matched clause carries NO finding signal (``_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE``) — so a real attribution
+# such as "prepared by the OECD, which found unemployment rose 2%" is KEPT (fail-open). Default-ON;
+# ``PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP=0`` restores byte-identical legacy text.
+_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP_ENV = "PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP"
+
+# Fixed-token furniture — excised unconditionally (never carries a finding).
+_INLINE_GOVBANNER_RE = re.compile(
+    r"An official website of the United States government\.?", re.IGNORECASE
+)
+_INLINE_CROSSREF_RE = re.compile(r"\bCrossref\s+\d+")
+_INLINE_READTIME_RE = re.compile(r"\b\d+\s+Minute\s+Read\s+Time\b", re.IGNORECASE)
+_INLINE_WP_NUMBER_RE = re.compile(r"\bWP/\d+/\d+\b")
+# A standalone dd-mm-yyyy / mm-dd-yyyy date stamp (scrape furniture). A real finding never renders a
+# figure in this hyphenated calendar-stamp form, so removing it never drops a finding number.
+_INLINE_DATESTAMP_RE = re.compile(r"\b\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}\b")
+
+# Clause-form front-matter — excised ONLY when the matched clause carries no finding signal (fail-open).
+_INLINE_IMF_COPYRIGHT_RE = re.compile(
+    r"©\s*\d{0,4}\s*International Monetary Fund", re.IGNORECASE
+)
+_INLINE_PREPARED_RE = re.compile(r"\bPrepared by\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?", re.IGNORECASE)
+_INLINE_AUTHORIZED_RE = re.compile(
+    r"\bAuthorized for distribution by\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?", re.IGNORECASE
+)
+_INLINE_ACK_RE = re.compile(
+    r"(?:\b(?:the\s+authors?|we|i)\s+)?would\s+like\s+to\s+thank\b[^.!?\n]*[.!?]?",
+    re.IGNORECASE,
+)
+_INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE = re.compile(r"^[\s,;:.\-–—]+")
+_INLINE_WS_RUN_RE = re.compile(r"[ \t]{2,}")
+
+
+def _inline_furniture_strip_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => the inline strip never runs =>
+    byte-identical legacy text. Mirrors the ``_snap_span_enabled`` off-token convention."""
+    return os.getenv(_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
+
+
+def _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx: "re.Pattern[str]", text: str) -> str:
+    """Remove every match of ``rx`` from ``text`` UNLESS the matched clause itself carries a finding
+    signal (a decimal / percentage / finding verb) — in which case the clause is a real attribution and
+    is KEPT untouched (fail-open). Pure."""
+    def _repl(m: "re.Match[str]") -> str:
+        frag = m.group(0)
+        if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(frag):
+            return frag  # a real finding is welded to the phrase — keep it whole
+        return " "
+    return rx.sub(_repl, text)
+
+
+def strip_inline_furniture(text: Any) -> str:
+    """Excise fixed boilerplate FRAGMENTS from inside a kept unit while keeping the surrounding clause
+    (I-deepfix-006 A/B). SUPPRESS-only, faithfulness-neutral: it can only remove furniture text, never
+    fabricate. Byte-identical to the input when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
+    if not _inline_furniture_strip_enabled():
+        return str(text or "")
+    s = str(text or "")
+    if not s.strip():
+        return s
+    # Fixed-token furniture: excised unconditionally (never a finding).
+    for rx in (
+        _INLINE_GOVBANNER_RE,
+        _INLINE_CROSSREF_RE,
+        _INLINE_READTIME_RE,
+        _INLINE_WP_NUMBER_RE,
+        _INLINE_DATESTAMP_RE,
+    ):
+        s = rx.sub(" ", s)
+    # Clause-form front-matter: excised only when the clause carries no finding signal (fail-open).
+    for rx in (
+        _INLINE_IMF_COPYRIGHT_RE,
+        _INLINE_PREPARED_RE,
+        _INLINE_AUTHORIZED_RE,
+        _INLINE_ACK_RE,
+    ):
+        s = _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx, s)
+    # Tidy whitespace + orphan leading punctuation left by a removed prefix fragment.
+    s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
+    return s.strip()
+
+
+# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# I-deepfix-006 C (#1376) — INLINE markup strip (SPAN-LEVEL, suppress-only). Removes raw render markup a
+# strict_verify-passing unit can carry: a "](http…)" markdown-link remnant, a bare URL, a bare URL-path
+# fragment with a query string ("/search/researchers?query=*&page=1"), an orphan markdown heading
+# ("## 2"), and a stray emphasis marker ("_**"). Over-stripping markup is faithfulness-safe — a URL /
+# heading marker / emphasis token is never a finding number or word. Default-ON; PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP=0
+# restores byte-identical legacy text.
+_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV = "PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP"
+_INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE = re.compile(r"\]\(https?://[^)]*\)")
+_INLINE_BARE_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://\S+")
+# A bare URL-PATH query fragment ("/search/researchers?institution=41ILO_INST&query=*&page=1"): a "/"
+# path carrying a "?...=" query param. Requiring the "=" avoids matching real prose like "what/why?".
+_INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE = re.compile(r"(?<![\w])/[^\s)\]]*\?[^\s)\]]*=[^\s)\]]*")
+# An orphan markdown heading welded MID-line ("… adoption grew. ## 2 firms invested") — the leading
+# ``(?<=\S)`` guard means a REAL numbered header at line start ("## 2 Results") is NEVER matched.
+_INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r"(?<=\S)\s+#{1,6}\s+\d+(?=\s|$)")
+_INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE = re.compile(r"_\*\*|\*\*_")
+
+
+def _inline_markup_strip_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy text."""
+    return os.getenv(_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
+
+
+def strip_inline_markup(text: Any) -> str:
+    """Excise raw render-markup fragments (markdown-link remnants, bare URLs / URL-path query fragments,
+    orphan markdown headings, stray emphasis markers) while keeping the surrounding prose. SUPPRESS-only,
+    faithfulness-neutral. Byte-identical when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
+    if not _inline_markup_strip_enabled():
+        return str(text or "")
+    s = str(text or "")
+    if not s.strip():
+        return s
+    s = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
+    return s.strip()
+
+
+# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# I-deepfix-006 D (#1376) — SHELL-SOURCE input screen (held out of the generator's drafting INPUT; the
+# source STAYS in the pool + bibliography + disclosure — never deleted). A "shell" source is one whose
+# direct_quote is DOMINATED by bracketed empty-anchor markdown links ("[](…)") and/or search-query URLs
+# with NO finding sentence (ev_716 = a pure nav/search link-farm). Its honest meta-description
+# ("The span consists of a repository collection link …") self-entails its own span and PASSES
+# strict_verify, so it must be screened at the drafting INPUT. A per-unit narration-detector belt also
+# withholds a shell-narration sentence lifted into an otherwise-real source. Default-ON;
+# PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN=0 restores byte-identical legacy behaviour.
+_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV = "PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN"
+_SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE = re.compile(r"\[\]\(")
+_SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE = re.compile(
+    r"/search\b|[?&](?:query|q|page|institution|search)=|query=\*", re.IGNORECASE
+)
+_SHELL_NARRATION_RE = re.compile(
+    r"the\s+span\s+consists\s+of|repository\s+collection\s+link|"
+    r"search\s+query\s+for\s+all\s+results",
+    re.IGNORECASE,
+)
+# Once the bracketed empty-anchor links and URLs are removed, a shell has very little real prose left.
+_SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS = 40
+
+
+def _shell_source_input_screen_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Kill-switch PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy."""
+    return os.getenv(_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
+
+
+def _is_shell_narration(text: Any) -> bool:
+    """True iff a unit is SHELL NARRATION — a meta-description of a nav/search link-farm ("The span
+    consists of …", "repository collection link", "search query for all results"). Pure."""
+    return bool(_SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(str(text or "")))
+
+
+def is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote: Any) -> bool:
+    """True iff a source's whole ``direct_quote`` is a nav/search SHELL — dominated by bracketed
+    empty-anchor markdown links and/or search-query URLs, carrying NO finding sentence and almost no
+    real prose once the link/URL scaffolding is removed. FAIL-CLOSED to KEEP (return False) on anything
+    ambiguous: a quote carrying a finding signal, or one with substantial residual prose, is NEVER a
+    shell. Pure — the source is only held out of drafting INPUT, never dropped from the pool."""
+    if not _shell_source_input_screen_enabled():
+        return False
+    s = str(direct_quote or "")
+    if not s.strip():
+        return False
+    # A real finding sentence anywhere => never a shell (fail-open to KEEP).
+    if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s):
+        return False
+    empty_anchors = len(_SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.findall(s))
+    has_search_url = bool(_SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE.search(s))
+    if empty_anchors < 1 and not has_search_url and not _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
+        return False  # no link-farm / search / narration signature at all => not a shell
+    # Measure residual prose after stripping the link/URL scaffolding: a shell has almost none.
+    residual = _SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.sub(" ", s)
+    residual = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", residual)
+    residual = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", residual)
+    residual = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", residual)
+    residual = _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.sub(" ", residual)
+    residual_alpha = "".join(ch for ch in residual if ch.isalpha() or ch.isspace()).strip()
+    # Dominated by link/URL scaffolding + shell narration, with little real prose left => a shell.
+    if (empty_anchors >= 2) or (empty_anchors >= 1 and has_search_url) or _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
+        return len(residual_alpha) < _SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS
+    return False
+
+
+# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# I-deepfix-006 E (#1376) — EVIDENCE-BASE finding-signal PREFERENCE (a §-1.3 WEIGHT/PLACEMENT: DEMOTE
+# to the low-relevance ledger, NEVER a drop). An on-topic marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal
+# (Thompson Rivers "top 10 predictions for 2025", AACSB "is leading the way in business education")
+# self-entails its own span and passes strict_verify, polluting the "Evidence base" body. Because such a
+# source is credible + on-topic (§-1.3: never deleted, only weighted), E DEMOTES it BELOW the appendix
+# boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — it STAYS in the pool, bibliography,
+# and disclosure. The demotion is a LAST-RESORT leg in ``_row_routes_to_ledger``: it fires ONLY for an
+# UNJUDGED source (no positive judged relevance label, no numeric selection_relevance) whose representative
+# text carries no finding signal — a real judge that SAW the content (rules 1/4) always wins. Default-ON;
+# PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE=0 removes the leg => byte-identical legacy routing.
+_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV = "PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE"
+
+
+def _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled() -> bool:
+    """Kill-switch PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE (default ON). OFF / empty => the ledger-routing
+    leg never fires => byte-identical legacy body/ledger partition."""
+    return os.getenv(_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in (
+        "0", "false", "off", "no",
+    )
+
+
+def _row_is_marketing_only_preamble(text: Any) -> bool:
+    """True iff ``text`` is a marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal (no decimal / percentage /
+    finding verb) — the TRU/AACSB shape. A demotion signal for an UNJUDGED row only; NEVER a drop.
+    FAIL-OPEN to KEEP (False) on empty text or when the kill-switch is OFF. Pure."""
+    if not _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled():
+        return False
+    s = str(text or "").strip()
+    if not s:
+        return False
+    return not bool(_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s))
+

 def partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger(
     rows: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
 ) -> "tuple[list[Any], list[Any]]":
     """Split ordered ``rows`` into ``(body, ledger)`` by JUDGED weight/relevance then FURNITURE/off-
     topic, ordering EACH partition by ``weight * relevance`` DESC. §-1.3 PLACEMENT, NEVER a drop:
 
       * ``body``   — rows kept in the report's carry-up prose (on-topic, at/above judged floor).
       * ``ledger`` — rows MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at
         weight)" section: furniture, confirmed-off-topic, judged-below-floor, or (unjudged) lexically
         off-topic. STILL present in the pool, bibliography, and disclosure — nothing is dropped.
 
     CONSERVATION (asserted by the caller's test): ``body`` and ``ledger`` are disjoint and their union
     equals ``rows`` (deduped by identity of order) — no row vanishes, none is duplicated. When the
     kill-switch is OFF, every row stays in ``body`` (byte-identical). PURE; no faithfulness touch.
 
     SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3): this row-list form is the general/reusable variant the unit tests exercise.
     The pipeline's raw carry-up surfaces are all ev-id ORDERED (weight order the render relies on), so
     the SHIPPED production entry is the order-preserving ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` —
     which shares the SAME per-row ``_row_routes_to_ledger`` verdict as this function."""

     if not low_relevance_ledger_enabled() or not row_list:
         return row_list, []
     q_terms = _placement_topic_terms(research_question)
     floor = _ledger_relevance_floor()
     body: list[Any] = []
     ledger: list[Any] = []
     for row in row_list:
         (ledger if _row_routes_to_ledger(row, q_terms, floor) else body).append(row)

 def _is_scaffolding_section_title(title: str) -> bool:
     """True iff a header title names a pipeline SCAFFOLDING section (excluded from sanitization)."""
     low = title.strip().lower().lstrip("# ").strip()

 def _line_has_claim_prose(line: str) -> bool:
     """True iff ``line`` carries claim-bearing prose (not just blanks or bare ``[N]`` /
     ``[#ev:...]`` citation markers). Strips leading bullet / ``**bold**`` markers and ALL citation
     markers, then checks any real alphabetic content remains. I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1 helper: used
     to decide whether a sanitized section body has collapsed to orphaned markers only. PURE."""
     text_only = "".join(_CITATION_SPLIT_RE.split(line)[::2])  # even indices = non-marker text
     return bool(_unit_core_for_screen(text_only).strip())
 
 
 def _immediate_parent_is_scaffolding(level: int, header_stack: "list[tuple[int, bool]]") -> bool:
     """True iff the NEAREST strictly-shallower open header (the immediate markdown parent) is a
     scaffolding header — e.g. ``### references`` whose parent is ``## Bibliography``. A non-scaffolding
     header at an intermediate depth BREAKS the chain (it becomes the new parent), so a content section
     under a non-scaffolding parent is NOT protected even if a far ancestor is the report's scaffolding
     ``# Research Report:`` title. ``header_stack`` holds ``(level, is_scaffolding)`` for the open
     ancestor headers, shallowest-first. PURE."""
     for anc_level, anc_scaffolding in reversed(header_stack):
         if anc_level < level:
             return anc_scaffolding
     return False

     the sentence unit and survives strict_verify's re-split (see ``_TERMINAL_PUNCT``).
     Accepts a single id (str) or an ordered list of ids; the order is preserved
     (representative first) and is deterministic.
     """
     if isinstance(eids, str):
         ids = [eids]
     else:
         ids = [str(e) for e in (eids or []) if str(e)]
     core = unit.rstrip()
     while core and core[-1] in _TERMINAL_PUNCT:
         core = core[:-1].rstrip()
     marker_str = "".join(f" [{eid}]" for eid in ids)
     return f"{core}{marker_str}."
 
 
 def _substantive_units(direct_quote: str, *, is_junk: Any) -> list[str]:
     """The source's verbatim sentence-units that are citable claims, longest-first.
 
     Splits with the SAME ``split_into_sentences`` strict_verify re-splits with, so
     each emitted unit is one gate unit. Keeps a unit only if it clears
     ``_MIN_UNIT_CHARS``, carries a real letter, is NOT boilerplate/chrome per the
     shared ``is_junk`` screen, and carries no ``[...]`` (which would be mis-read as a
     marker). Ordered longest-first so the per-source budget keeps the most
     content-bearing sentences (most likely the real finding).
     """
     from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
         split_into_sentences,
     )
 
     max_chars = max_unit_chars()
+    # I-deepfix-006 D (#1376): a nav/search SHELL source (dominated by empty-anchor links / search-query
+    # URLs, no finding sentence — ev_716) is held OUT of the drafting INPUT. The source stays in the
+    # pool + bibliography + disclosure; only its verbatim spans are withheld from drafting. Default-ON;
+    # byte-identical when PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN=0 (``is_shell_source_quote`` returns False).
+    if is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote):
+        return []
     units: list[str] = []
     for raw_unit in split_into_sentences(direct_quote) or []:
         # I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289): strip C0 control bytes (incl. a literal NUL) from
         # the unit BEFORE any length/screen check so a control byte can never reach the
         # render and the bound measures clean printable chars.
         unit = _strip_control_bytes(raw_unit or "").strip()
+        # I-deepfix-006 A/B/C (#1376): excise fixed boilerplate furniture fragments + raw markup from
+        # INSIDE the unit while keeping the surrounding clause. Suppress-only, faithfulness-neutral;
+        # byte-identical when both kill-switches are OFF.
+        unit = strip_inline_furniture(unit)
+        unit = strip_inline_markup(unit)
+        # I-deepfix-006 D (#1376): withhold a per-unit shell-narration sentence ("The span consists of …",
+        # "repository collection link", "search query for all results") lifted into an otherwise-real source.
+        if _shell_source_input_screen_enabled() and _is_shell_narration(unit):
+            continue
         if len(unit) < _MIN_UNIT_CHARS:
             continue
         # I-beatboth-011 #4 (#1289): a unit longer than the render bound is structurally
         # a fetch-shell / raw-extraction blob (the 75K equation dump), never a clinical
         # sentence — DROP it. NOT a breadth cap (source count uncapped); NOT a verify
         # gate (strict_verify untouched). A real long quote is sentence-split upstream.
         if len(unit) > max_chars:
             continue
         if not any(ch.isalpha() for ch in unit):
             continue
         # `[...]`-shaped substrings inside a quote would be mis-read as markers
         # by _rewrite_draft_with_spans; a unit carrying one is skipped (rare; keeps
         # the marker contract unambiguous rather than risk a false token bind).
         if "[" in unit and "]" in unit:
             continue
         if is_junk(unit):
             continue
         units.append(unit)
     units.sort(key=len, reverse=True)
     return units
 
 
 # I-beatboth-011 #7 (#1289) — SAME-WORK CONSOLIDATION identity (§-1.3 CONSOLIDATE-
 # DON'T-DROP). Two unbound SUPPORTS members are the SAME WORK when they share a
 # normalized DOI, else a folded title PLUS a corroborating discriminator. KEEP ALL
 # their URLs as corroborating locators of the ONE work, but COUNT/PRESENT them as ONE
 # source (multi-URL corroboration), never N independent sources. Identity ladder
 # mirrors the existing ``_m51_canonical_identity`` convention (evidence_selector.py:
 # 2781): DOI first, else title(+discriminator), else (fallback) the evidence_id itself
 # so a member with neither stays its own distinct unit (never wrongly merged).

 3537: def _inline_furniture_strip_enabled() -> bool:
 3538:     """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => the inline strip never runs =>
 3539:     byte-identical legacy text. Mirrors the ``_snap_span_enabled`` off-token convention."""
 3540:     return os.getenv(_INLINE_FURNITURE_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")

 3543: def _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx: "re.Pattern[str]", text: str) -> str:
 3544:     """Remove every match of ``rx`` from ``text`` UNLESS the matched clause itself carries a finding
 3545:     signal (a decimal / percentage / finding verb) — in which case the clause is a real attribution and
 3546:     is KEPT untouched (fail-open). Pure."""
 3547:     def _repl(m: "re.Match[str]") -> str:
 3548:         frag = m.group(0)
 3549:         if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(frag):
 3550:             return frag  # a real finding is welded to the phrase — keep it whole
 3551:         return " "
 3552:     return rx.sub(_repl, text)
 3553: 
 3554: 
 3555: def strip_inline_furniture(text: Any) -> str:
 3556:     """Excise fixed boilerplate FRAGMENTS from inside a kept unit while keeping the surrounding clause
 3557:     (I-deepfix-006 A/B). SUPPRESS-only, faithfulness-neutral: it can only remove furniture text, never
 3558:     fabricate. Byte-identical to the input when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
 3559:     if not _inline_furniture_strip_enabled():
 3560:         return str(text or "")
 3561:     s = str(text or "")
 3562:     if not s.strip():
 3563:         return s
 3564:     # Fixed-token furniture: excised unconditionally (never a finding).
 3565:     for rx in (
 3566:         _INLINE_GOVBANNER_RE,
 3567:         _INLINE_CROSSREF_RE,
 3568:         _INLINE_READTIME_RE,
 3569:         _INLINE_WP_NUMBER_RE,
 3570:         _INLINE_DATESTAMP_RE,
 3571:     ):
 3572:         s = rx.sub(" ", s)
 3573:     # Clause-form front-matter: excised only when the clause carries no finding signal (fail-open).
 3574:     for rx in (
 3575:         _INLINE_IMF_COPYRIGHT_RE,
 3576:         _INLINE_PREPARED_RE,
 3577:         _INLINE_AUTHORIZED_RE,
 3578:         _INLINE_ACK_RE,
 3579:     ):
 3580:         s = _strip_clause_if_no_finding(rx, s)
 3581:     # Tidy whitespace + orphan leading punctuation left by a removed prefix fragment.
 3582:     s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3583:     s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
 3584:     return s.strip()
 3585: 
 3586: 
 3587: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 3588: # I-deepfix-006 C (#1376) — INLINE markup strip (SPAN-LEVEL, suppress-only). Removes raw render markup a
 3589: # strict_verify-passing unit can carry: a "](http…)" markdown-link remnant, a bare URL, a bare URL-path
 3590: # fragment with a query string ("/search/researchers?query=*&page=1"), an orphan markdown heading
 3591: # ("## 2"), and a stray emphasis marker ("_**"). Over-stripping markup is faithfulness-safe — a URL /
 3592: # heading marker / emphasis token is never a finding number or word. Default-ON; PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP=0
 3593: # restores byte-identical legacy text.
 3594: _INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV = "PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP"
 3595: _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE = re.compile(r"\]\(https?://[^)]*\)")
 3596: _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://\S+")
 3597: # A bare URL-PATH query fragment ("/search/researchers?institution=41ILO_INST&query=*&page=1"): a "/"
 3598: # path carrying a "?...=" query param. Requiring the "=" avoids matching real prose like "what/why?".
 3599: _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE = re.compile(r"(?<![\w])/[^\s)\]]*\?[^\s)\]]*=[^\s)\]]*")
 3600: # An orphan markdown heading welded MID-line ("… adoption grew. ## 2 firms invested") — the leading
 3601: # ``(?<=\S)`` guard means a REAL numbered header at line start ("## 2 Results") is NEVER matched.
 3602: _INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r"(?<=\S)\s+#{1,6}\s+\d+(?=\s|$)")
 3603: _INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE = re.compile(r"_\*\*|\*\*_")
 3604: 
 3605: 
 3606: def _inline_markup_strip_enabled() -> bool:
 3607:     """Kill-switch PG_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy text."""
 3608:     return os.getenv(_INLINE_MARKUP_STRIP_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
 3609: 
 3610: 
 3611: def strip_inline_markup(text: Any) -> str:
 3612:     """Excise raw render-markup fragments (markdown-link remnants, bare URLs / URL-path query fragments,
 3613:     orphan markdown headings, stray emphasis markers) while keeping the surrounding prose. SUPPRESS-only,
 3614:     faithfulness-neutral. Byte-identical when the kill-switch is OFF or nothing matches. Pure."""
 3615:     if not _inline_markup_strip_enabled():
 3616:         return str(text or "")
 3617:     s = str(text or "")
 3618:     if not s.strip():
 3619:         return s
 3620:     s = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3621:     s = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3622:     s = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3623:     s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_HEADING_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3624:     s = _INLINE_STRAY_EMPHASIS_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3625:     s = _INLINE_WS_RUN_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3626:     s = _INLINE_ORPHAN_LEAD_RE.sub("", s)
 3627:     return s.strip()
 3628: 
 3629: 
 3630: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 3631: # I-deepfix-006 D (#1376) — SHELL-SOURCE input screen (held out of the generator's drafting INPUT; the
 3632: # source STAYS in the pool + bibliography + disclosure — never deleted). A "shell" source is one whose
 3633: # direct_quote is DOMINATED by bracketed empty-anchor markdown links ("[](…)") and/or search-query URLs
 3634: # with NO finding sentence (ev_716 = a pure nav/search link-farm). Its honest meta-description
 3635: # ("The span consists of a repository collection link …") self-entails its own span and PASSES
 3636: # strict_verify, so it must be screened at the drafting INPUT. A per-unit narration-detector belt also
 3637: # withholds a shell-narration sentence lifted into an otherwise-real source. Default-ON;
 3638: # PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN=0 restores byte-identical legacy behaviour.
 3639: _SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV = "PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN"
 3640: _SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE = re.compile(r"\[\]\(")
 3641: _SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE = re.compile(
 3642:     r"/search\b|[?&](?:query|q|page|institution|search)=|query=\*", re.IGNORECASE
 3643: )
 3644: _SHELL_NARRATION_RE = re.compile(
 3645:     r"the\s+span\s+consists\s+of|repository\s+collection\s+link|"
 3646:     r"search\s+query\s+for\s+all\s+results",
 3647:     re.IGNORECASE,
 3648: )
 3649: # Once the bracketed empty-anchor links and URLs are removed, a shell has very little real prose left.
 3650: _SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS = 40
 3651: 
 3652: 
 3653: def _shell_source_input_screen_enabled() -> bool:
 3654:     """Kill-switch PG_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN (default ON). OFF / empty => byte-identical legacy."""
 3655:     return os.getenv(_SHELL_SOURCE_INPUT_SCREEN_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
 3656: 
 3657: 
 3658: def _is_shell_narration(text: Any) -> bool:
 3659:     """True iff a unit is SHELL NARRATION — a meta-description of a nav/search link-farm ("The span
 3660:     consists of …", "repository collection link", "search query for all results"). Pure."""
 3661:     return bool(_SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(str(text or "")))
 3662: 
 3663: 
 3664: def is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote: Any) -> bool:
 3665:     """True iff a source's whole ``direct_quote`` is a nav/search SHELL — dominated by bracketed
 3666:     empty-anchor markdown links and/or search-query URLs, carrying NO finding sentence and almost no
 3667:     real prose once the link/URL scaffolding is removed. FAIL-CLOSED to KEEP (return False) on anything
 3668:     ambiguous: a quote carrying a finding signal, or one with substantial residual prose, is NEVER a
 3669:     shell. Pure — the source is only held out of drafting INPUT, never dropped from the pool."""
 3670:     if not _shell_source_input_screen_enabled():
 3671:         return False
 3672:     s = str(direct_quote or "")
 3673:     if not s.strip():
 3674:         return False
 3675:     # A real finding sentence anywhere => never a shell (fail-open to KEEP).
 3676:     if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s):
 3677:         return False
 3678:     empty_anchors = len(_SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.findall(s))
 3679:     has_search_url = bool(_SHELL_SEARCH_URL_RE.search(s))
 3680:     if empty_anchors < 1 and not has_search_url and not _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
 3681:         return False  # no link-farm / search / narration signature at all => not a shell
 3682:     # Measure residual prose after stripping the link/URL scaffolding: a shell has almost none.
 3683:     residual = _SHELL_EMPTY_ANCHOR_RE.sub(" ", s)
 3684:     residual = _INLINE_MDLINK_REMNANT_RE.sub(" ", residual)
 3685:     residual = _INLINE_BARE_URL_RE.sub(" ", residual)
 3686:     residual = _INLINE_URL_PATH_QUERY_RE.sub(" ", residual)
 3687:     residual = _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.sub(" ", residual)
 3688:     residual_alpha = "".join(ch for ch in residual if ch.isalpha() or ch.isspace()).strip()
 3689:     # Dominated by link/URL scaffolding + shell narration, with little real prose left => a shell.
 3690:     if (empty_anchors >= 2) or (empty_anchors >= 1 and has_search_url) or _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.search(s):
 3691:         return len(residual_alpha) < _SHELL_RESIDUAL_PROSE_MIN_CHARS
 3692:     return False
 3693: 
 3694: 
 3695: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 3696: # I-deepfix-006 E (#1376) — EVIDENCE-BASE finding-signal PREFERENCE (a §-1.3 WEIGHT/PLACEMENT: DEMOTE
 3697: # to the low-relevance ledger, NEVER a drop). An on-topic marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal
 3698: # (Thompson Rivers "top 10 predictions for 2025", AACSB "is leading the way in business education")
 3699: # self-entails its own span and passes strict_verify, polluting the "Evidence base" body. Because such a
 3700: # source is credible + on-topic (§-1.3: never deleted, only weighted), E DEMOTES it BELOW the appendix
 3701: # boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — it STAYS in the pool, bibliography,
 3702: # and disclosure. The demotion is a LAST-RESORT leg in ``_row_routes_to_ledger``: it fires ONLY for an
 3703: # UNJUDGED source (no positive judged relevance label, no numeric selection_relevance) whose representative
 3704: # text carries no finding signal — a real judge that SAW the content (rules 1/4) always wins. Default-ON;
 3705: # PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE=0 removes the leg => byte-identical legacy routing.
 3706: _EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV = "PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE"
 3707: 
 3708: 
 3709: def _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled() -> bool:
 3710:     """Kill-switch PG_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE (default ON). OFF / empty => the ledger-routing
 3711:     leg never fires => byte-identical legacy body/ledger partition."""
 3712:     return os.getenv(_EVIDENCE_BASE_FINDING_PREFERENCE_ENV, "1").strip().lower() not in (
 3713:         "0", "false", "off", "no",
 3714:     )
 3715: 
 3716: 
 3717: def _row_is_marketing_only_preamble(text: Any) -> bool:
 3718:     """True iff ``text`` is a marketing PREAMBLE with no finding signal (no decimal / percentage /
 3719:     finding verb) — the TRU/AACSB shape. A demotion signal for an UNJUDGED row only; NEVER a drop.
 3720:     FAIL-OPEN to KEEP (False) on empty text or when the kill-switch is OFF. Pure."""
 3721:     if not _evidence_base_finding_preference_enabled():
 3722:         return False
 3723:     s = str(text or "").strip()
 3724:     if not s:
 3725:         return False
 3726:     return not bool(_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s))
 3727: 
 3728: 
 3729: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 3730: # I-deepfix-001 F2 (#1371) — UNIFIED BODY-PLACEMENT SCREEN + Low-relevance ledger partition.
 3731: #
 3732: # THE BUG (Fable F2 root cause): a grammatical sentence ABOUT junk (page furniture that renders as a
 3733: # coherent line, or an on-topic-looking sentence that is actually off the research question's topic)
 3734: # self-entails its own verbatim span, so it PASSES the frozen strict_verify gate and survives into the
 3735: # raw carry-up surfaces (Verified Findings / Abstract / Key Findings / Conclusion / Evidence base /
 3736: # CWF facet sections). Those surfaces have a FORM-chrome screen (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable``)
 3737: # but NO topicality screen. Meanwhile the pipeline ALREADY computes per-row judged relevance
 3738: # (``selection_relevance`` + the W2 ``content_relevance_label``) that these seams ignore.
 3739: #
 3740: # THE FIX — §-1.3 WEIGHT / PLACEMENT, NEVER DELETE: make body PLACEMENT respect the weight already
 3741: # computed. A unit that is FURNITURE or confidently OFF-topic is MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into
 3742: # a clearly-labelled "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — it STAYS in the evidence pool,
 3743: # the bibliography, and the disclosure; nothing is dropped, capped, or thinned. The frozen faithfulness
 3744: # engine (strict_verify / NLI / 4-role D8 / provenance / span-grounding) is UNTOUCHED. The topicality
 3745: # leg reuses the EXISTING grounding tokenizer (``provenance_generator._content_words``) — no new model.
 3746: #
 3747: # SHIPPED SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3, resolving the dual-gate scope-wiring finding): the ledger PLACEMENT is
 3748: # wired into the two EV-ID-ordered raw carry-up surfaces — the "Evidence base" breadth section AND the
 3749: # weighted-enrichment "Corroborated Weighted Findings" (CWF) facet/flat sections — via the SINGLE
 3750: # order-preserving production entry ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` (both surfaces consume
 3751: # its BODY partition; the ledger rows render once below the appendix; see multi_section_generator.py at
 3752: # the CWF plan-build seam + assembly). The Verified Findings / Abstract / Key Findings / Conclusion
 3753: # surfaces are SYNTHESIZED PROSE, not ev-id lists, and stay covered by the pre-existing FORM-chrome +
 3754: # strict_verify screen; F2 does NOT retrofit a topicality screen onto synthesized prose in this ship.
 3755: # ``is_offtopic_or_chrome_for_placement`` (the unified TEXT predicate) and
 3756: # ``partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger`` (the row-list form) are the general/reusable forms the
 3757: # unit tests exercise directly; they share the SAME ``_row_routes_to_ledger`` / furniture / topicality
 3758: # core that ships to production through ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger``.
 3759: _OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_WORDS = 6  # a zero-overlap unit this long is confidently off-topic; below it,
 3760: #                                    only a unit ALSO carrying no finding signal is demoted (fail-open).
 3761: 
 3762: # Report-INSTRUCTION scaffolding words (deliverable-format vocabulary, NOT topic). A verbose benchmark
 3763: # question ("write a COMPREHENSIVE research REPORT drawing on credible SOURCES … with COLUMNS …") is
 3764: # laden with these; if they stay in the topical reference an off-topic intruder that merely says
 3765: # "publication"/"comprehensive"/"analysis" escapes the topicality demotion. Stripping them from the
 3766: # PLACEMENT reference ONLY (never from the production ``_question_topic_terms`` the ordering/promotion/
 3767: # span gates use) sharpens the lexical FALLBACK without touching any live ordering. Domain-agnostic
 3768: # (these describe the deliverable, not any field), fail-open (an over-strip keeps a source in body,
 3769: # never a drop — §-1.3). The clearly-topical words (impact, employment, occupation, industry, risk,
 3770: # …) are deliberately NOT here.
 3771: #
 3772: # Codex F2 gate iter-1 (HC-5 P2): the plausibly-TOPICAL words are pruned OUT of this set so they stay
 3773: # as live topic terms — ``evidence``, ``literature``, ``application(s)``, ``area(s)``, ``case(s)``,
 3774: # ``country/countries``, ``region(s)``, ``view(s)``, ``example(s)``, ``detail(s)``. In a grants /
 3775: # bibliometrics / geography / privacy report those ARE the topic, so stripping them could have
 3776: # over-routed a real on-topic source to the ledger when one of them was its only shared term. They are
 3777: # NOT deliverable-only words. Only the unambiguous deliverable-FORMAT vocabulary remains below.
 3778: _REPORT_SCAFFOLDING_TERMS = frozenset({
 3779:     "publication", "comprehensive", "analysis", "report", "reports", "research", "researching",
 3780:     "source", "sources", "provide", "provides", "summary", "summarizing", "table", "tables",
 3781:     "column", "columns", "section", "sections", "structure", "specific", "specifically",
 3782:     "key", "main", "detailing", "drawing", "please", "write", "written", "available", "credible",
 3783:     "relevant", "restriction", "date", "dates", "type", "types", "aspect", "aspects",
 3784:     "particular", "regarding", "limitation", "limitations", "support",
 3785:     "supporting", "end", "separate",
 3786: })
 3787: 
 3788: 
 3789: def _placement_topic_terms(research_question: str) -> frozenset[str]:
 3790:     """The PLACEMENT topical reference: ``_question_topic_terms`` minus the report-instruction
 3791:     scaffolding words. Used ONLY by the F2 body-placement predicate + ledger routing so the noisy
 3792:     lexical FALLBACK is sharpened; the production ordering/promotion/span gates keep the full
 3793:     ``_question_topic_terms`` (byte-identical). Empty question => empty set => fail-open (keep-all)."""
 3794:     return frozenset(_question_topic_terms(research_question)) - _REPORT_SCAFFOLDING_TERMS
 3795: 
 3796: 
 3797: def _is_offtopic_for_placement(text: Any, question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]") -> bool:
 3798:     """True iff a grammatical unit is confidently OFF the research question's topic — a PLACEMENT
 3799:     demotion signal, NEVER a drop. FAIL-OPEN (return False => keep in body) whenever: there are no
 3800:     question terms (empty/blank research question => every legacy caller is byte-identical), the unit
 3801:     carries no content words, or the unit shares ANY content word with the question. A unit with ZERO
 3802:     question overlap is off-topic only when it is long enough to judge (``>= _OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_
 3803:     WORDS`` content words) OR — for a terse unit — it ALSO carries no finding signal (a real terse
 3804:     finding carries a percentage / decimal / finding verb, so it is never demoted here). PURE."""
 3805:     if not question_terms:
 3806:         return False
 3807:     try:
 3808:         from src.polaris_graph.generator.provenance_generator import (  # noqa: PLC0415
 3809:             _content_words,
 3810:         )
 3811:         unit_terms = _content_words(str(text or ""))
 3812:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-safe: a tokenizer/import failure must never DEMOTE a real
 3813:         return False  #                    source to the ledger (§-1.3 fail-open, mirrors _ledger_relevance_floor)
 3814:     if not unit_terms:
 3815:         return False
 3816:     if unit_terms & set(question_terms):
 3817:         return False  # any shared topic term => on-topic, KEEP in body
 3818:     if len(unit_terms) >= _OFFTOPIC_PLACEMENT_MIN_WORDS:
 3819:         return True   # long, zero-overlap => confidently foreign to the question
 3820:     # terse + zero-overlap: demote only when it also lacks a finding signal (guard a real terse finding)
 3821:     return not bool(_FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(str(text or "")))
 3822: 
 3823: 
 3824: def is_offtopic_or_chrome_for_placement(text: Any, *, research_question: str = "") -> bool:
 3825:     """The unified F2 BODY-PLACEMENT screen. True iff a grammatical, strict_verify-passable unit is
 3826:     page/source FURNITURE (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` — the FORM screen, honouring its
 3827:     ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` kill-switch) OR confidently OFF the research question's topic
 3828:     (``_is_offtopic_for_placement`` — the topicality screen this seam previously lacked).
 3829: 
 3830:     A True verdict routes the unit BELOW the appendix boundary into the labelled "Low-relevance
 3831:     evidence (kept at weight)" ledger — a §-1.3 PLACEMENT demotion, NEVER a drop / cap / thin. The
 3832:     source stays in the pool, the bibliography, and the disclosure. The faithfulness engine is
 3833:     untouched. FAIL-OPEN for the topicality leg on an empty research question (byte-identical legacy).
 3834: 
 3835:     The FORM leg is the shared ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate PLUS the F2 placement-only
 3836:     furniture vocabulary (``_contains_f2_placement_furniture``) — the F2 vocab lives on the PLACEMENT
 3837:     path only, never on the shared drop predicate (Codex F2 iter-1 HC-2).
 3838: 
 3839:     SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3): this unified TEXT predicate is the general/reusable form the unit tests
 3840:     exercise directly. The SHIPPED production placement is the order-preserving, judged-relevance-aware
 3841:     ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` (wired into both ev-id carry-up surfaces: Evidence base +
 3842:     CWF), which shares this predicate's furniture + topicality legs via ``_row_routes_to_ledger``."""
 3843:     if is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(text) or _contains_f2_placement_furniture(text):
 3844:         return True
 3845:     return _is_offtopic_for_placement(text, _placement_topic_terms(research_question))
 3846: 
 3847: 
 3848: # ── Low-relevance ledger: the labelled below-the-appendix partition (§-1.3 PLACEMENT, never a drop) ──
 3849: _LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER_TITLE = "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)"
 3850: _ENV_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER = "PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER"  # default ON
 3851: 
 3852: 
 3853: def low_relevance_ledger_enabled() -> bool:
 3854:     """Kill-switch ``PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER`` (default ON). OFF => the ledger partition never fires
 3855:     => every row stays in the body order => byte-identical to the legacy single-surface render."""
 3856:     return os.environ.get(_ENV_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER, "1").strip().lower() not in (
 3857:         "0", "false", "no", "off",
 3858:     )
 3859: 
 3860: 
 3861: def _ledger_relevance_floor() -> float:
 3862:     """The judged-relevance floor for the body/ledger split — the SAME ``PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR`` the
 3863:     retrieval + enrichment gates use (default 0.30), with its fail-loud (0.0, 1.0] validation. A row
 3864:     whose JUDGED ``selection_relevance`` sits below this is routed to the ledger (placement, not a
 3865:     drop). Lazy import keeps this module import-time independent of the retrieval side."""
 3866:     try:
 3867:         from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.evidence_selector import (  # noqa: PLC0415
 3868:             parse_relevance_floor,
 3869:         )
 3870:         return parse_relevance_floor(os.environ.get("PG_RELEVANCE_FLOOR"))
 3871:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — fail-safe default; a broken import must never crash placement
 3872:         return 0.30
 3873: 
 3874: 
 3875: def _ledger_row_text(row: Any) -> str:
 3876:     """The render text a placement screen should judge: the member's direct quote / statement, else a
 3877:     join of the standard topic text fields. PURE read; never a faithfulness touch."""
 3878:     if not isinstance(row, dict):
 3879:         return ""
 3880:     quote = _member_quote(row)
 3881:     if quote:
 3882:         return quote
 3883:     return " ".join(str(row.get(f) or "") for f in _TOPIC_TEXT_FIELDS).strip()
 3884: 
 3885: 
 3886: def _ledger_weight_relevance_key(row: Any) -> "tuple[float, float]":
 3887:     """The ``(weight, relevance)`` ordering key (both DESC when negated by the caller). Reads the
 3888:     row's basket ``weight_mass`` (else ``credibility_weight``/``weight``) and its judged
 3889:     ``selection_relevance`` (missing => the keep-neutral sentinel). Ordering only — never a filter."""
 3890:     weight = 0.0
 3891:     for field in ("weight_mass", "credibility_weight", "weight"):
 3892:         raw = row.get(field) if isinstance(row, dict) else None
 3893:         if raw is not None:
 3894:             try:
 3895:                 weight = float(raw)
 3896:                 break
 3897:             except (TypeError, ValueError):
 3898:                 continue
 3899:     rel = _row_relevance(row)
 3900:     return (weight, _relevance_sort_key(rel))
 3901: 
 3902: 
 3903: def _row_routes_to_ledger(
 3904:     row: Any, question_terms: "frozenset[str] | set[str]", relevance_floor: float
 3905: ) -> bool:
 3906:     """Per-row body-vs-ledger verdict. POSITIVE judged relevance FIRST, then furniture, then the rest
 3907:     (Codex F2 gate iter-1 P1: positive-relevance-first ordering):
 3908:       1. A POSITIVE judged ``content_relevance_label`` (relevant / escalated_relevant) => BODY. A real
 3909:          upstream judge that SAW the content wins over every heuristic leg (§-1.3 WEIGHT-not-FILTER), so
 3910:          a judged-relevant row whose text incidentally trips a broad furniture regex is NOT demoted.
 3911:       2. FURNITURE (``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` OR the F2 placement-only vocab
 3912:          ``_contains_f2_placement_furniture``) => ledger. The F2 vocab lives on the PLACEMENT path only,
 3913:          never on the shared drop predicate (HC-2); a match is a placement (move to the ledger), never a
 3914:          drop — the source stays in the pool + bibliography + disclosure.
 3915:       3. A confirmed-OFF judged label (``topic_offtopic_demoted`` True or a demoted/escalated_demoted
 3916:          ``content_relevance_label``) => ledger.
 3917:       4. A JUDGED numeric ``selection_relevance`` below the floor => ledger (placement, not a drop).
 3918:       5. NO judgment => fall back to lexical question-term overlap (``_is_offtopic_for_placement``).
 3919:     PURE read of already-computed state; the faithfulness engine is untouched."""
 3920:     label = ""
 3921:     if isinstance(row, dict):
 3922:         label = str(row.get("content_relevance_label", "") or "").strip().lower()
 3923:     if label in _POSITIVE_RELEVANCE_LABELS:
 3924:         return False  # judged relevant => ALWAYS body (positive-relevance-first; never buried)
 3925:     text = _ledger_row_text(row)
 3926:     if is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(text) or _contains_f2_placement_furniture(text):
 3927:         return True  # furniture => ledger (placement, never a drop; F2 vocab never feeds a drop seam)
 3928:     if not isinstance(row, dict):
 3929:         return False
 3930:     if row.get("topic_offtopic_demoted") is True or label in _CONFIRMED_OFFTOPIC_LABELS:
 3931:         return True
 3932:     rel = _row_relevance(row)
 3933:     if rel is not None:
 3934:         return rel < relevance_floor  # judged below-floor => ledger (placement)
 3935:     # Unjudged: lexical off-topic => ledger.
 3936:     if _is_offtopic_for_placement(text, question_terms):
 3937:         return True
 3938:     # I-deepfix-006 E (#1376): an UNJUDGED marketing-only preamble (no finding signal — TRU/AACSB) is
 3939:     # DEMOTED to the ledger (kept at weight, never a drop). A real judge (rules 1/4) always wins first.
 3940:     if _row_is_marketing_only_preamble(text):
 3941:         return True
 3942:     return False
 3943: 
 3944: 
 3945: def partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger(
 3946:     rows: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
 3947: ) -> "tuple[list[Any], list[Any]]":
 3948:     """Split ordered ``rows`` into ``(body, ledger)`` by JUDGED weight/relevance then FURNITURE/off-
 3949:     topic, ordering EACH partition by ``weight * relevance`` DESC. §-1.3 PLACEMENT, NEVER a drop:
 3950: 
 3951:       * ``body``   — rows kept in the report's carry-up prose (on-topic, at/above judged floor).
 3952:       * ``ledger`` — rows MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into the "Low-relevance evidence (kept at
 3953:         weight)" section: furniture, confirmed-off-topic, judged-below-floor, or (unjudged) lexically
 3954:         off-topic. STILL present in the pool, bibliography, and disclosure — nothing is dropped.
 3955: 
 3956:     CONSERVATION (asserted by the caller's test): ``body`` and ``ledger`` are disjoint and their union
 3957:     equals ``rows`` (deduped by identity of order) — no row vanishes, none is duplicated. When the
 3958:     kill-switch is OFF, every row stays in ``body`` (byte-identical). PURE; no faithfulness touch.
 3959: 
 3960:     SCOPE (F2 gate iter-3): this row-list form is the general/reusable variant the unit tests exercise.
 3961:     The pipeline's raw carry-up surfaces are all ev-id ORDERED (weight order the render relies on), so
 3962:     the SHIPPED production entry is the order-preserving ``partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger`` —
 3963:     which shares the SAME per-row ``_row_routes_to_ledger`` verdict as this function."""
 3964:     row_list = list(rows or [])
 3965:     if not low_relevance_ledger_enabled() or not row_list:
 3966:         return row_list, []
 3967:     q_terms = _placement_topic_terms(research_question)
 3968:     floor = _ledger_relevance_floor()
 3969:     body: list[Any] = []
 3970:     ledger: list[Any] = []
 3971:     for row in row_list:
 3972:         (ledger if _row_routes_to_ledger(row, q_terms, floor) else body).append(row)
 3973: 
 3974:     def _order(partition: list[Any]) -> list[Any]:
 3975:         # Stable weight*relevance DESC (a demotion order, never a filter). Index tiebreak preserves the
 3976:         # caller's incoming order within an equal-key group so the sort is deterministic.
 3977:         indexed = list(enumerate(partition))
 3978:         indexed.sort(
 3979:             key=lambda pair: (
 3980:                 -(lambda wr: wr[0] * wr[1])(_ledger_weight_relevance_key(pair[1])),
 3981:                 pair[0],
 3982:             )
 3983:         )
 3984:         return [row for _, row in indexed]
 3985: 
 3986:     return _order(body), _order(ledger)
 3987: 
 3988: 
 3989: def partition_evidence_base_ids_for_ledger(
 3990:     ev_ids: Any, evidence_pool: Any, *, research_question: str = ""
 3991: ) -> "tuple[list[str], list[str]]":
 3992:     """Order-PRESERVING split of the ordered Evidence-base ``ev_ids`` into ``(body, ledger)`` using the
 3993:     same per-row body/ledger verdict as ``partition_body_and_low_relevance_ledger``.
 3994: 
 3995:     The incoming order (already weight*relevance from ``select_unbound_supports_by_weight``) is
 3996:     PRESERVED within each partition — the render (``build_evidence_base_section``) relies on that
 3997:     order, so this NEVER re-sorts. A ledger id is FURNITURE / confirmed-off-topic / judged-below-floor
 3998:     / (unjudged) lexically off-topic — it is MOVED BELOW the appendix boundary into the labelled
 3999:     "Low-relevance evidence (kept at weight)" section, and STAYS in the pool + bibliography + disclosure
 4000:     (§-1.3 PLACEMENT, never a drop). A pool-absent id stays in ``body`` (the render skips it exactly as
 4001:     before — no placement change for a non-resolvable id). Conservation: ``body`` + ``ledger`` equals
 4002:     the de-duplicated non-empty input. OFF (``PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER=0``) => ``(list(ev_ids), [])``."""
 4003:     # HC-7 (Codex F2 iter-1 P2): the OFF check is FIRST, before any dedup / empty-strip, so a
 4004:     # PG_LOW_RELEVANCE_LEDGER=0 run feeds the body section the ORIGINAL ids untouched — strictly
 4005:     # byte-identical to legacy even when duplicate / empty ids are present in the input.
 4006:     #
 4007:     # F2 gate iter-6 (Codex NOVEL P0 — decoupled-flag placement-becomes-DROP): the ledger partition is
 4008:     # RENDERED only through ``build_evidence_base_section`` — BOTH the Evidence base body AND the ledger
 4009:     # section are gated internally by ``PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION``. If that flag is OFF the ledger
 4010:     # section CANNOT render, so routing rows into it while the CWF body-feed (multi_section_generator)
 4011:     # consumes only the body partition would make those rows vanish from the report prose AND the
 4012:     # bibliography — a §-1.3 DROP. COUPLE the split to the render gate: when the Evidence base surface
 4013:     # cannot render, the split returns ``(full-surface, [])`` so every row stays in the body order (fed
 4014:     # to CWF), the ledger is empty, and PG_BREADTH_EVIDENCE_BASE_SECTION=0 stays byte-identical to legacy
 4015:     # (its documented kill-switch contract). The move-half NEVER fires without the place-half.
 4016:     if not low_relevance_ledger_enabled() or not evidence_base_section_enabled():
 4017:         return list(ev_ids or []), []
 4018:     ids: list[str] = []
 4019:     seen: set[str] = set()
 4020:     for e in (ev_ids or []):
 4021:         e = str(e or "")
 4022:         if e and e not in seen:
 4023:             seen.add(e)
 4024:             ids.append(e)
 4025:     if not ids:
 4026:         return list(ev_ids or []), []
 4027:     pool = evidence_pool or {}
 4028:     q_terms = _placement_topic_terms(research_question)
 4029:     floor = _ledger_relevance_floor()
 4030:     body: list[str] = []
 4031:     ledger: list[str] = []
 4032:     for eid in ids:
 4033:         row = pool.get(eid)
 4034:         if not isinstance(row, dict):
 4035:             body.append(eid)  # pool-absent => leave in body; the render skips it as before (no change)
 4036:             continue
 4037:         (ledger if _row_routes_to_ledger(row, q_terms, floor) else body).append(eid)
 4038:     return body, ledger

 4042: # I-wire-012 (#1326) — FAIL-LOUD chrome-as-claim CANARY on the SHIPPED report.
 4043: #
 4044: # A render-integrity tripwire: it measures what FRACTION of the report's CLAIM bullets
 4045: # are chrome (page furniture that rendered as a finding) and, in ``enforce`` mode above
 4046: # a floor, REFUSES to ship — so a chrome regression can NOT ship as
 4047: # ``released_with_disclosed_gaps``. It NEVER promotes a unit and NEVER touches a
 4048: # faithfulness verdict. Modes (LAW VI, default-safe):
 4049: #   off     — explicit opt-out: no telemetry, no enforce.
 4050: #   warn    — emit telemetry to the manifest; never fails the run.
 4051: #   enforce — DEFAULT (I-wire-013 #1327): emit telemetry AND fail the run (status flip) when rate > floor.
 4052: _RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY"
 4053: _RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR_ENV = "PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY_FLOOR"
 4054: _DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_FLOOR = 0.05
 4055: _RENDER_CANARY_MODES = ("off", "warn", "enforce")
 4056: _DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_MODE = "enforce"
 4057: 
 4058: # A TOP-LEVEL report bullet (no leading indent) = a claim surface (Key-Findings, the
 4059: # per-claim corroboration header, a finding bullet). Indented ``  - SUPPORT:`` /
 4060: # ``  - GROUNDED-BUT-WEAK`` sub-bullets (source URLs, not claims) and numbered
 4061: # bibliography lines ("1. Title") are deliberately EXCLUDED so the rate measures
 4062: # chrome-as-CLAIM, not chrome-as-source-locator.
 4063: _TOP_LEVEL_BULLET_RE = re.compile(r"^-\s+(.*\S)\s*$")
 4064: _BOLD_MARKER_RE = re.compile(r"\*\*")

 4067: def render_chrome_canary_mode() -> str:
 4068:     """Canary mode from ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_CANARY`` (off|warn|enforce); default ``enforce``
 4069:     (I-wire-013 #1327 — the tripwire enforces by default, not telemetry-only). Fail-loud on an
 4070:     UNRECOGNIZED value (LAW II — no silent guessed fallback), mirroring ``render_chrome_canary_floor``.
 4071:     ``off`` is the explicit opt-out (telemetry suppressed by the caller; verdict never trips)."""
 4072:     raw = os.environ.get(_RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV)
 4073:     if raw is None or not raw.strip():
 4074:         return _DEFAULT_RENDER_CANARY_MODE
 4075:     mode = raw.strip().lower()
 4076:     if mode not in _RENDER_CANARY_MODES:
 4077:         raise ValueError(
 4078:             f"{_RENDER_CANARY_MODE_ENV}={raw!r} is not a valid chrome-canary mode "
 4079:             f"(expected one of {_RENDER_CANARY_MODES})"
 4080:         )
 4081:     return mode

 4531: def _sanitize_report_line(line: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None") -> "tuple[str, int]":
 4532:     """Sanitize ONE claim-section body line: split it into per-``[N]`` citation units, drop each unit
 4533:     (with its own trailing marker) that is chrome or a corpus-grounded truncation cut, and repair a
 4534:     unit that is real prose with a glued inline header. Returns ``(clean_line, dropped_count)``. A
 4535:     marker-less unit that is the whole short line is dropped iff it is chrome (a standalone ToC /
 4536:     masthead line). PURE."""
 4537:     parts = _CITATION_SPLIT_RE.split(line)
 4538:     segments: list[tuple[str, str]] = []
 4539:     i = 0
 4540:     while i < len(parts):
 4541:         seg_text = parts[i]
 4542:         seg_marker = parts[i + 1] if i + 1 < len(parts) else ""
 4543:         segments.append((seg_text, seg_marker))
 4544:         i += 2
 4545:     kept: list[str] = []
 4546:     dropped = 0
 4547:     # I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX B: when a prose segment is dropped as chrome, the SAME claim's trailing
 4548:     # continuation citation markers ("prose[6][7][5]" splits into a prose seg + two marker-only segs)
 4549:     # would otherwise survive orphaned. Track the drop and suppress the contiguous marker-only run
 4550:     # that immediately follows it. A marker-only run after a KEPT segment stays (it belongs to that
 4551:     # kept claim). Withhold-only — the dropped markers' evidence is untouched.
 4552:     suppress_trailing_markers = False
 4553:     for seg_text, seg_marker in segments:
 4554:         if not seg_text.strip() and not seg_marker:
 4555:             continue
 4556:         # A marker-only continuation segment (no prose, just "[N]") inherits the fate of the prose
 4557:         # segment it continues: dropped if that prose segment was dropped, kept otherwise.
 4558:         if not seg_text.strip():
 4559:             if suppress_trailing_markers:
 4560:                 dropped += 1
 4561:                 continue
 4562:             kept.append(seg_text + seg_marker)
 4563:             continue
 4564:         core = _unit_core_for_screen(seg_text)
 4565:         if core and is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable(core, known_words=known_words):
 4566:             repaired = _repair_glued_inline_header(seg_text, known_words)
 4567:             if repaired is not None:
 4568:                 # Real-prose prefix kept WITH its citation marker (the kept finding stays cited);
 4569:                 # only the glued-header remainder is excised. The prose survives, so its trailing
 4570:                 # continuation markers are NOT orphaned — keep them.
 4571:                 kept.append(repaired + seg_marker)
 4572:                 dropped += 1
 4573:                 suppress_trailing_markers = False
 4574:                 continue
 4575:             dropped += 1
 4576:             suppress_trailing_markers = True  # orphan this dropped claim's continuation markers
 4577:             continue  # whole chrome unit + its marker dropped
 4578:         kept.append(seg_text + seg_marker)
 4579:         suppress_trailing_markers = False
 4580:     # I-deepfix-001 H1 (#1344): REPAIR-first strip of leaked source-internal in-text ref markers
 4581:     # ("(1, 2)") on the kept prose. No-op (byte-identical) when the kill-switch is OFF or the line
 4582:     # carries no such marker; never touches the report's OWN ``[N]`` / ``[#ev:...]`` square-bracket
 4583:     # markers (they are seg_marker parts, and the rule matches PARENTHESES only). Faithfulness-neutral.
 4584:     # I-deepfix-006 A/B/C (#1376): also excise fixed boilerplate furniture fragments + raw markup that
 4585:     # were welded INSIDE the kept prose. Suppress-only; byte-identical when both kill-switches are OFF.
 4586:     cleaned = strip_source_internal_refs("".join(kept))
 4587:     cleaned = strip_inline_furniture(cleaned)
 4588:     cleaned = strip_inline_markup(cleaned)
 4589:     return cleaned, dropped

 4592: def _is_scaffolding_section_title(title: str) -> bool:
 4593:     """True iff a header title names a pipeline SCAFFOLDING section (excluded from sanitization)."""
 4594:     low = title.strip().lower().lstrip("# ").strip()
 4595:     return any(low.startswith(s) for s in _SCAFFOLDING_SECTION_TITLES)

 4598: def _line_has_claim_prose(line: str) -> bool:
 4599:     """True iff ``line`` carries claim-bearing prose (not just blanks or bare ``[N]`` /
 4600:     ``[#ev:...]`` citation markers). Strips leading bullet / ``**bold**`` markers and ALL citation
 4601:     markers, then checks any real alphabetic content remains. I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1 helper: used
 4602:     to decide whether a sanitized section body has collapsed to orphaned markers only. PURE."""
 4603:     text_only = "".join(_CITATION_SPLIT_RE.split(line)[::2])  # even indices = non-marker text
 4604:     return bool(_unit_core_for_screen(text_only).strip())

 4607: def _immediate_parent_is_scaffolding(level: int, header_stack: "list[tuple[int, bool]]") -> bool:
 4608:     """True iff the NEAREST strictly-shallower open header (the immediate markdown parent) is a
 4609:     scaffolding header — e.g. ``### references`` whose parent is ``## Bibliography``. A non-scaffolding
 4610:     header at an intermediate depth BREAKS the chain (it becomes the new parent), so a content section
 4611:     under a non-scaffolding parent is NOT protected even if a far ancestor is the report's scaffolding
 4612:     ``# Research Report:`` title. ``header_stack`` holds ``(level, is_scaffolding)`` for the open
 4613:     ancestor headers, shallowest-first. PURE."""
 4614:     for anc_level, anc_scaffolding in reversed(header_stack):
 4615:         if anc_level < level:
 4616:             return anc_scaffolding
 4617:     return False

 4619: 
 4620: def _drop_empty_claim_sections(lines: "list[str]") -> "tuple[list[str], int]":
 4621:     """I-wire-017 (#1339) FIX C1 post-pass: drop a non-scaffolding ``###``-or-deeper section header
 4622:     whose body — after the line-level sanitization already ran — has NO claim-bearing prose left
 4623:     (only blank lines / bare orphaned citation markers). Such a section renders as a dangling header
 4624:     over "[6][7][5]"; withholding the empty header is suppress-only (the evidence is untouched).
 4625: 
 4626:     A SCAFFOLDING header — by its own title OR by having a scaffolding IMMEDIATE parent
 4627:     (``### references`` under ``## Bibliography``) — is always preserved. Any top-level (``#``/``##``)
 4628:     header is also preserved (a top-level empty section is left for the operator). Returns
 4629:     ``(kept_lines, headers_dropped)``. PURE."""
 4630:     kept: list[str] = []
 4631:     headers_dropped = 0
 4632:     # Open ancestor headers as (level, is_scaffolding), shallowest-first; a header at depth d closes
 4633:     # every open ancestor at depth >= d before it is pushed.
 4634:     header_stack: list[tuple[int, bool]] = []
 4635:     i = 0
 4636:     n = len(lines)
 4637:     while i < n:
 4638:         header = _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(lines[i])
 4639:         if not header:
 4640:             kept.append(lines[i])
 4641:             i += 1
 4642:             continue
 4643:         level = len(header.group(1))
 4644:         title = header.group(2)
 4645:         parent_scaffolding = _immediate_parent_is_scaffolding(level, header_stack)
 4646:         header_stack = [hs for hs in header_stack if hs[0] < level]
 4647:         own_scaffolding = _is_scaffolding_section_title(title)
 4648:         header_stack.append((level, own_scaffolding))
 4649:         if (
 4650:             level < _MIN_DROPPABLE_EMPTY_HEADER_LEVEL
 4651:             or own_scaffolding
 4652:             or parent_scaffolding
 4653:         ):
 4654:             kept.append(lines[i])
 4655:             i += 1
 4656:             continue
 4657:         # Collect this section's body up to (not including) the next header of ANY level.
 4658:         body_start = i + 1
 4659:         j = body_start
 4660:         while j < n and not _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(lines[j]):
 4661:             j += 1
 4662:         body = lines[body_start:j]
 4663:         if any(_line_has_claim_prose(b) for b in body):
 4664:             kept.extend(lines[i:j])  # real content survives -> keep header + body verbatim
 4665:         else:
 4666:             headers_dropped += 1  # empty content section -> drop header + its marker-only body
 4667:         i = j
 4668:     return kept, headers_dropped

 4671: def sanitize_rendered_report(
 4672:     report_md: str, known_words: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None" = None
 4673: ) -> "tuple[str, int]":
 4674:     """THE render-seam chokepoint (I-wire-013 #1327). Run ONE sanitization pass over every
 4675:     claim-bearing unit of the assembled ``report_md``, dropping/repairing chrome + truncated units
 4676:     with the unblinded ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable`` predicate. Returns
 4677:     ``(clean_report_md, units_removed)``.
 4678: 
 4679:     Scaffolding sections (Bibliography / Methods / disclosures / Reliability / Source corroboration /
 4680:     the H1 question echo) are byte-preserved. A glued-chrome HEADER line ("## Dennis Zami …" welded
 4681:     onto a title) is dropped; a clean section header is preserved. Default-ON kill-switch
 4682:     ``PG_RENDER_SEAM_SANITIZE``; faithfulness-neutral (suppress-only). PURE."""
 4683:     if not report_md or not render_seam_sanitize_enabled():
 4684:         return report_md, 0
 4685:     out_lines: list[str] = []
 4686:     removed = 0
 4687:     in_scaffolding = False
 4688:     # I-deepfix-001 B6(a): tracked SEPARATELY from in_scaffolding. The corroboration section is
 4689:     # scaffolding (byte-preserved DOIs/URLs) EXCEPT its per-claim HEADER bullets, which carry a
 4690:     # claim string that can be page-furniture chrome. When in_corroboration is set and the B6(a)
 4691:     # screen is enabled, header bullets are screened; sub-bullets stay byte-preserved (KEEP-ONLY).
 4692:     in_corroboration = False
 4693:     corroboration_screen = corroboration_sanitize_enabled()
 4694:     # I-deepfix-001 H2 (#1344): tracked separately — inside the flat/residual "Corroborated Weighted
 4695:     # Findings" enrichment section, split the glued single-paragraph body into one bullet per finding.
 4696:     in_enrichment = False
 4697:     cwf_split = cwf_split_findings_enabled()
 4698:     for line in report_md.split("\n"):
 4699:         header = _SECTION_HEADER_RE.match(line)
 4700:         if header:
 4701:             title = header.group(2)
 4702:             in_scaffolding = _is_scaffolding_section_title(title)
 4703:             in_corroboration = _is_corroboration_section_title(title)
 4704:             in_enrichment = _is_enrichment_section_title(title)
 4705:             # Screen a glued-chrome header by its TITLE (post-``#`` strip), but never a clean /
 4706:             # scaffolding header — dropping a real header would orphan its body. Gated by
 4707:             # ``render_chrome_screen_enabled()`` so this header path honours the same
 4708:             # ``PG_RENDER_CHROME_SCREEN=0`` kill-switch as ``is_render_chrome_or_unrenderable``
 4709:             # (Codex P1 iter 1: the direct ``_contains_forensic_chrome`` call otherwise bypassed it).
 4710:             if (
 4711:                 not in_scaffolding
 4712:                 and render_chrome_screen_enabled()
 4713:                 and _contains_forensic_chrome(title)
 4714:             ):
 4715:                 removed += 1
 4716:                 continue
 4717:             out_lines.append(line)
 4718:             continue
 4719:         if in_corroboration and corroboration_screen and line.strip():
 4720:             # B6(a): inside the corroboration rollup, screen ONLY the per-claim HEADER bullet's
 4721:             # claim string (sub-bullets / blanks pass through untouched via the (line, 0) branch).
 4722:             clean_line, suppressed = _sanitize_corroboration_header(line, known_words)
 4723:             removed += suppressed
 4724:             out_lines.append(clean_line)
 4725:             continue
 4726:         if in_scaffolding or not line.strip():
 4727:             out_lines.append(line)
 4728:             continue
 4729:         if in_enrichment and cwf_split:
 4730:             # H2: de-blob the enrichment section — split the glued ``sentence.[N] sentence.[N] ...``
 4731:             # paragraph into one bullet per finding, each sanitized through the SAME per-line screen
 4732:             # and keeping ONLY its own trailing ``[N]`` marker. Faithfulness-neutral render reflow.
 4733:             bullet_lines, dropped = _split_enrichment_blob_line(line, known_words)
 4734:             removed += dropped
 4735:             out_lines.extend(bullet_lines)
 4736:             continue
 4737:         clean_line, dropped = _sanitize_report_line(line, known_words)
 4738:         removed += dropped
 4739:         if clean_line.strip() or not dropped:
 4740:             out_lines.append(clean_line)
 4741:         # else: the line reduced entirely to chrome -> drop the now-empty line.
 4742:     # I-deepfix-001 (drb_72) FIX-D belt: after the line-level pass, drop any surviving bullet that is
 4743:     # ONLY a list marker and/or orphan citation markers ("- ", "- [12]") — it carries no claim. A real
 4744:     # bibliography line ("1. Title") never matches (it is not a ``-``/``*`` bullet). SUPPRESS-ONLY.
 4745:     _empty_bullet_drop = empty_bullet_drop_enabled()
 4746:     if _empty_bullet_drop:

 4794:         core = core[:-1].rstrip()

 3664: def is_shell_source_quote(direct_quote: Any) -> bool:
 3665:     """True iff a source's whole ``direct_quote`` is a nav/search SHELL — dominated by bracketed
 3666:     empty-anchor markdown links and/or search-query URLs, carrying NO finding sentence and almost no
 3667:     real prose once the link/URL scaffolding is removed. FAIL-CLOSED to KEEP (return False) on anything
 3668:     ambiguous: a quote carrying a finding signal, or one with substantial residual prose, is NEVER a
 3669:     shell. Pure — the source is only held out of drafting INPUT, never dropped from the pool."""
 3670:     if not _shell_source_input_screen_enabled():
 3671:         return False
 3672:     s = str(direct_quote or "")
 3673:     if not s.strip():
 3674:         return False
 3675:     # A real finding sentence anywhere => never a shell (fail-open to KEEP).
 3676:     if _FINDING_SIGNAL_RE.search(s):
 3677:         return False

 3687:     residual = _SHELL_NARRATION_RE.sub(" ", residual)
 3688:     residual_alpha = "".join(ch for ch in residual if ch.isalpha() or ch.isspace()).strip()

codex
The span-cleaning layer has one real over-strip issue: the date-stamp regex is unconditional and runs on general rendered claim lines, not only a prefix stamp. It removes legitimate hyphenated dates from substantive policy/reporting claims, producing broken prose.  def _snap_span_end_to_sentence(haystack: str, start: int, end: int) -> int:
     """EXTEND ``end`` forward to just past the next REAL sentence terminator in ``haystack`` when the
     cited span ends mid-sentence. Extend-ONLY (never shrinks) -> the result is always a SUPERSET of the
     original span within the SAME row. Returns ``end`` unchanged when the span already ends at a
     boundary, when no REAL terminator is found within the bounded scan (avoid running to EOF), or on
     any out-of-range input (fail-safe no-op). A decimal point / abbreviation dot is NOT a terminator
     (Codex #1335 gate P1) so the snap can never truncate a number to its integer part."""
     if not haystack:
         return end
     n = len(haystack)
     if not (0 <= start < end <= n):
         return end
     if _ends_at_sentence_boundary(haystack, end):
         return end
     try:
         max_extend = int(os.getenv(_ENV_SNAP_MAX_EXTEND_CHARS, "").strip() or _DEFAULT_SNAP_MAX_EXTEND_CHARS)
     except ValueError:
         max_extend = _DEFAULT_SNAP_MAX_EXTEND_CHARS
     max_extend = max(1, max_extend)
     limit = min(n, end + max_extend)
     for i in range(end, limit):
         if _is_real_sentence_terminator(haystack, i, n):
             j = i + 1
             if j < n and haystack[j] in "\"')]":
                 j += 1
             return j
     return end
 
 
+# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# I-deepfix-006 F (#1376) — FULL-QUOTE-WINDOW SNAP (the P0 truncated-number fix).
+#
+# THE BUG (drb_72): a verified span byte-range whose START or END lands MID-VALUE (the extractor cut the
+# member's direct_quote at "…exposure rises to 4" from "…46%", or at "6% of tasks" from "46%…") composes
+# a garbled clause with a truncated number/word. This SNAPS both window ends against the evidence-pool
+# row's FULL direct_quote at window-mining time, so a number/word is never cut mid-value.
+#
+# Extend-ONLY within the SAME row => a SUPERSET of the verified span => grounded by construction (the
+# emitted text is a verbatim slice of the row; strict_verify re-checks the whole number is present in
+# both sentence and span). Bounded so a pathological token can never swallow the row. Default-ON;
+# PG_FULL_QUOTE_WINDOW_SNAP=0 restores byte-identical legacy behaviour.
+_ENV_FULL_QUOTE_WINDOW_SNAP = "PG_FULL_QUOTE_WINDOW_SNAP"
+# A whole "value" token: a number (with decimal / thousands separators + a trailing %) OR an alphabetic
+# word. Matching these lets the snap recognise a mid-value cut ("46%", "3.75", "reinstatement").
+_WHOLE_VALUE_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\d[\d.,]*%?|[^\W\d_]+")
+_MAX_WHOLE_VALUE_EXTEND = 64  # cap the per-end extension so a runaway token can never swallow the row
+
+
+def _full_quote_window_snap_enabled() -> bool:
+    """PG_FULL_QUOTE_WINDOW_SNAP gate (mirrors ``_snap_span_enabled``): default-ON; only an explicit
+    0/false/off/no disables. An EMPTY string behaves like UNSET (stays ON)."""
+    return os.getenv(_ENV_FULL_QUOTE_WINDOW_SNAP, "1").strip().lower() not in ("0", "false", "off", "no")
+
+
+def _snap_window_to_whole_value(haystack: str, start: int, end: int) -> "tuple[int, int]":
+    """Snap ``(start, end)`` outward to whole-value token boundaries in ``haystack`` so neither end cuts
+    a number or word mid-value. Extend-ONLY (the result is a SUPERSET within the same row); bounded by
+    ``_MAX_WHOLE_VALUE_EXTEND`` per end; a no-op on out-of-range input. Pure."""
+    n = len(haystack)
+    if not haystack or not (0 <= start < end <= n):
+        return start, end
+    new_start, new_end = start, end
+    for m in _WHOLE_VALUE_TOKEN_RE.finditer(haystack):
+        ms, me = m.start(), m.end()
+        if ms < start < me:
+            new_start = min(new_start, ms)
+        if ms < end < me:
+            new_end = max(new_end, me)
+        if ms >= end:
+            break  # tokens are ordered; nothing past ``end`` can contain ``start`` or ``end``
+    # Bound each extension so a pathological token can never swallow the row.
+    if start - new_start > _MAX_WHOLE_VALUE_EXTEND:
+        new_start = start
+    if new_end - end > _MAX_WHOLE_VALUE_EXTEND:
+        new_end = end
+    return new_start, new_end
+

+def _reformat_uncovered_disclosure(text: str) -> str:
+    """Rewrite one "[uncovered supporting evidence for: {subject}] {span}" block into human prose
+    ("Evidence was retrieved for the following claims but no span met the verification floor: {subject}.
+    {span}"). Returns ``text`` unchanged when the kill-switch is OFF or the text is not an uncovered-fact

+    if not m:

+    lead = _UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_HUMAN_LEAD + (subject or "this claim")
+    if not lead.endswith("."):
+        lead += "."
+    return f"{lead} {span}".strip() if span else lead
