 def _is_degraded_verify_disclosure_unit(text: Any) -> bool:
     """True iff a whole composed unit IS the degraded-verify disclosure placeholder (``[verification
     incomplete: ...]``). ``_compose_one_basket`` returns the disclosure ALONE for a no-verified-span
     basket (kept prose empty), so a pure-disclosure unit STARTS with the prefix; a mixed
     ``verified prose. [verification incomplete: ...]`` unit does NOT (it starts with the prose) and
     stays in the strict_verify-bound draft, preserving its verified prose."""
     return str(text or "").strip().lower().startswith(_DEGRADED_VERIFY_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX)
 
 
 def _is_no_verified_span_disclosure(text: Any) -> bool:
     """True iff ``text`` is EITHER no-verified-span disclosure placeholder — the legacy bare
     ``[insufficient verified evidence ...]`` gap OR the ARM-B ``[verification incomplete: ...]``
     degraded-verify label. Used by ``repair_untokened_sentence`` so NEITHER is ever rebound to a foreign
     SUPPORTS basket (a disclosure placeholder is not a claim; rebinding it is the P1a laundering bug)."""
     lowered = str(text or "").strip().lower()
     return (
         lowered.startswith(_INSUFFICIENT_EVIDENCE_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX)
         or lowered.startswith(_DEGRADED_VERIFY_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX)
     )
 
 
 def _is_composed_disclosure_paragraph(text: Any) -> bool:
     """True iff a composed paragraph is a HELD-ASIDE disclosure unit — the ARM-B degraded-verify label
     (``[verification incomplete: ...]``) OR the SYNTH_PRIMARY uncovered-fact label
     (``[uncovered supporting evidence for: ...]``). Both are routed aside by
     ``partition_composed_disclosures`` and re-appended after strict_verify. The uncovered-fact prefix is
     ONLY produced on the SYNTH_PRIMARY ON path, so this is byte-identical to the pre-Wave-1a
     degraded-only classification when PG_SYNTH_PRIMARY is OFF (no unit ever starts with it)."""
     lowered = str(text or "").strip().lower()
     return (
         _is_degraded_verify_disclosure_unit(text)
         or lowered.startswith(_UNCOVERED_FACT_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX)
     )

     unchanged (byte-identical)."""

     if not kept_disclosures:

 1277: # THE BUG (Codex Wave-3 P1a): the DISTINCT "[verification incomplete: ...]" label is emitted as TOKENLESS
 1278: # raw text by ``_compose_one_basket``. The legacy "[insufficient verified evidence]" marker is SUPPRESSED
 1279: # by ``_compose_section_per_basket`` (:1284) before it can leak, but the degraded label was NOT — so it
 1280: # flowed into the strict_verify-bound draft where (a) ``_repair_untokened_draft`` could REBIND its
 1281: # tokenless text to some other SUPPORTS basket (laundering an honest gap into a fabricated cited claim),
 1282: # or (b) ``strict_verify`` dropped it ``no_provenance_token`` (the honest label never reached output).
 1283: #
 1284: # THE CARRIER: recognize BOTH no-verified-span disclosure placeholders, HOLD the degraded label ASIDE
 1285: # before it enters the strict_verify-bound draft (``_run_section`` calls ``partition_composed_disclosures``),
 1286: # and RENDER it back onto the section body AFTER strict_verify + the render screens (``_run_section`` calls
 1287: # ``render_degraded_disclosures``). It never becomes verified prose (no ``[#ev]`` token, not in
 1288: # ``kept_sentences``, ``sentences_verified`` unchanged), and ``repair_untokened_sentence`` refuses to
 1289: # rebind it — so it is treated EXACTLY like the legacy insufficient-evidence disclosure by
 1290: # ``_repair_untokened_draft`` / ``strict_verify`` (never rebound, never dropped as garbage). It is a
 1291: # marker-less honest disclosure, the SAME faithfulness class as the section-level gap stub. Byte-identical
 1292: # when PG_DEGRADED_VERIFY_DISCLOSURE is OFF (no such label is ever produced => the partition is a no-op).
 1293: _INSUFFICIENT_EVIDENCE_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX = "[insufficient verified evidence"
 1294: _DEGRADED_VERIFY_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX = "[verification incomplete:"
 1295: # I-deepfix-001 Wave-1a (#1344) — the SYNTH_PRIMARY uncovered-fact labeled-disclosure prefix. When the
 1296: # bounded repair loop exhausts with a residual failing authored sentence, the basket's verbatim
 1297: # uncovered-fact K-span is emitted as a SEPARATE `[`-prefixed disclosure paragraph (redactor no-touch
 1298: # set: a line starting with `[` is never TIER-2 redacted) routed aside by ``partition_composed_disclosures``
 1299: # and re-appended AFTER strict_verify by ``render_degraded_disclosures`` — NEVER the mid-line
 1300: # `" ".join(kept + [fallback])` glue. It is a verbatim span (grounded by construction) rendered as an
 1301: # honest labeled block. ONLY produced on the SYNTH_PRIMARY ON path => byte-identical when OFF.
 1302: _UNCOVERED_FACT_DISCLOSURE_PREFIX = "[uncovered supporting evidence for:"
 1303: 
 1304: # I-deepfix-006 C3 (#1376) — REFORMAT the SYNTH_PRIMARY uncovered-fact disclosure into human prose at
 1305: # RENDER time. The block "[uncovered supporting evidence for: {subject}] {span}" is an INTENTIONAL honest
 1306: # disclosure (never a leak) but renders raw with brackets. This rewrites it to a readable sentence, NEVER
 1307: # deletes it. Applied ONLY at ``render_degraded_disclosures`` (after ``partition_composed_disclosures``
 1308: # has already routed the block aside by its ``[`` prefix), so the partition/classification is untouched.
 1309: # Default-ON; PG_UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_REFORMAT=0 keeps the raw bracket block byte-for-byte.
 1310: _ENV_UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_REFORMAT = "PG_UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_REFORMAT"
 1311: _UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_HUMAN_LEAD = (
 1312:     "Evidence was retrieved for the following claims but no span met the verification floor: "
 1313: )
 1314: _UNCOVERED_FACT_BLOCK_RE = re.compile(
 1315:     r"^\[uncovered supporting evidence for:\s*(?P<subject>.*?)\]\s*(?P<span>.*)$",
 1316:     re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL,
 1317: )
 1318: 
 1319: 
 1320: def _uncovered_disclosure_reformat_enabled() -> bool:
 1321:     """PG_UNCOVERED_DISCLOSURE_REFORMAT gate (default ON). OFF / empty => the raw bracket block renders
 1322:     byte-for-byte (legacy)."""

 1324:         "0", "false", "off", "no",

    4: furniture symbol (* © •, whitespace optional) or — with mandatory whitespace — a digit / opening quote,

    9: not a superlative claim. Both default-ON, byte-identical OFF.

   20: def test_split_before_glued_furniture_symbol():
   21:     out = pg.split_into_sentences("Adoption rose to 12%.* Bullet furniture here that is long.")
   22:     assert out == ["Adoption rose to 12%.", "* Bullet furniture here that is long."]
   23: 
   24: 
   25: def test_split_before_copyright_symbol():

   27:     assert out[0] == "The rate held steady."
   28:     assert out[1].startswith("© 2025 Publisher")

   34:

   37:     # "3.75" has no whitespace after the '.', so the digit leg must NOT split it.
   38:     assert pg.split_into_sentences("The rate rose to 3.75 percent overall.") == [
   39:         "The rate rose to 3.75 percent overall."
   40:     ]

   47: 
   48: 
   49: def test_glued_closing_quote_is_not_split_off():

   52:         'She said it was "done." Everyone agreed later.'
   53:     ]

  568: # I-deepfix-006 C5 — clean analyst-synthesis render (PG_SYNTH_RENDER_CLEAN, default ON)
  569: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  570: # De-clutters the rendered "Analyst Synthesis" block WITHOUT touching the frozen faithfulness engine
  571: # or any claim. Two render-only edits:
  572: #   (1) DEDUPE the DOUBLED disclosure. ``_apply_synthesis_deviation_screen`` prepends the
  573: #       ``ANALYST_SYNTHESIS_DISCLOSURE`` INTO ``analyst_synthesis_text`` whenever the analyst block
  574: #       renders, AND the sole report renderer (run_honest_sweep_r3.py ~L15436) ALSO emits that same
  575: #       disclosure as the italic "## Analyst Synthesis" section preamble. Result in report.md: the
  576: #       disclosure twice, back-to-back. This pass removes the IN-TEXT copy so the renderer's canonical
  577: #       preamble is the single one. The section STAYS labeled interpretive (the renderer always adds
  578: #       the preamble — it is the only consumer of ``analyst_synthesis_text`` — so the section is never
  579: #       left unlabeled).
  580: #   (2) LIFT the per-sentence ``[confidence: <bucket> — …]`` markers (appended by the B13/D3 deviation
  581: #       check via ``claim_labeler.render_confidence_marker``) OUT of the prose into ONE compact
  582: #       per-section confidence note (bucket counts). The section-level disclosure remains the binding
  583: #       honesty signal; no claim is upgraded, none dropped — the labels are aggregated, not discarded.
  584: # Faithfulness-neutral + render-only. Default-ON; OFF => byte-identical (returns the text unchanged);
  585: # ON with an already-clean block (no in-text disclosure, no markers) is also byte-identical.
  586: _RENDER_CLEAN_ENV = "PG_SYNTH_RENDER_CLEAN"
  587: _RENDER_CLEAN_OFF_VALUES = ("0", "false", "off", "no")
  588: # Mirrors analyst_synthesis_deviation_check._CONFIDENCE_MARKER_RE (leading whitespace + the bracket).
  589: _RENDER_CLEAN_CONF_MARKER_RE = re.compile(r"[ \t]*\[confidence:[^\]]*\]")
  590: # The bucket label is the first token after "[confidence:" up to the " — " separator; buckets are the
  591: # claim_labeler VALID_BUCKETS (high / moderate / low / no-source-found — lowercase, may carry hyphens).
  592: _RENDER_CLEAN_CONF_BUCKET_RE = re.compile(r"\[confidence:\s*([A-Za-z-]+)")
  593: _RENDER_CLEAN_BUCKET_ORDER = ("high", "moderate", "low", "no-source-found")
  594: 
  595: 
  596: def _render_clean_enabled() -> bool:
  597:     """C5 kill-switch. Default-ON; OFF only for an explicit off-value (byte-identical legacy render)."""
  598:     return (
  599:         os.environ.get(_RENDER_CLEAN_ENV, "1").strip().lower()
  600:         not in _RENDER_CLEAN_OFF_VALUES
  601:     )
  602: 
  603: 
  604: def _render_clean_synthesis(text: str) -> str:
  605:     """Return the render-cleaned analyst-synthesis text (C5). See module block above.
  606: 
  607:     Pure, no-network, faithfulness-neutral. Returns the input UNCHANGED when the flag is OFF or when
  608:     there is nothing to clean (no in-text disclosure copy AND no inline confidence markers)."""
  609:     if not text or not text.strip() or not _render_clean_enabled():
  610:         return text
  611:     had_disclosure = ANALYST_SYNTHESIS_DISCLOSURE in text
  612:     buckets = [b.lower() for b in _RENDER_CLEAN_CONF_BUCKET_RE.findall(text)]
  613:     if not had_disclosure and not buckets:
  614:         return text  # already clean -> byte-identical
  615:     cleaned = text
  616:     if had_disclosure:
  617:         # Remove EVERY in-text copy (guarded ≤1 upstream, but be defensive) — the renderer re-adds one.
  618:         cleaned = cleaned.replace(ANALYST_SYNTHESIS_DISCLOSURE, "")
  619:     if buckets:
  620:         cleaned = _RENDER_CLEAN_CONF_MARKER_RE.sub("", cleaned)
  621:     # Tidy whitespace the strips left behind (trailing spaces, >2 consecutive blank lines, leading blanks).
  622:     cleaned = re.sub(r"[ \t]+\n", "\n", cleaned)
  623:     cleaned = re.sub(r"\n{3,}", "\n\n", cleaned).lstrip("\n")
  624:     if buckets:
  625:         counts = Counter(buckets)
  626:         ordered = [f"{counts[b]} {b}" for b in _RENDER_CLEAN_BUCKET_ORDER if counts.get(b)]
  627:         for b in counts:  # any non-standard label -> keep it, appended after the known order
  628:             if b not in _RENDER_CLEAN_BUCKET_ORDER:
  629:                 ordered.append(f"{counts[b]} {b}")
  630:         note = (
  631:             "_Confidence labels for this interpretive section: "
  632:             + ", ".join(ordered)
  633:             + ". Each was a per-sentence groundedness check, summarized here; the whole section is "
  634:             "interpretive and not individually span-verified._"
  635:         )
  636:         cleaned = f"{note}\n\n{cleaned}" if cleaned.strip() else note
  637:     return cleaned

**Findings**

P0: C1 is not “strict_verify except lexical overlap.” The new entailment leg bypasses several hard faithfulness checks in the frozen verifier. In [synthesis_entailment_verify.py](C:/POLARIS/src/polaris_graph/synthesis/synthesis_entailment_verify.py:132), `_numbers_match` checks only decimal/integer subset membership before entailment. It does not preserve strict verifier gates such as percent-role matching, qualifier retention, trial-name matching, additive overstatement/unit/role/polarity guards, or cited-span shell rejection in [provenance_generator.py](C:/POLARIS/src/polaris_graph/generator/provenance_generator.py:2337). I reproduced a concrete failure: span text containing bare `15` kept the sentence `Employment rose 15% [#ev:...]` through `entailment_verify(..., entails_fn=True)`, while `strict_verify` dropped it with `percent_not_in_cited_span`. That means the union wrapper can add sentences the frozen engine rejects for non-lexical faithfulness reasons. This violates the central constraint that only the lexical >=2 content-word leg is replaced.

P1: Promote-only D8 routing can skip the depth true-drop reconcile when legacy D8 is off. [native_gate_b_inputs.py](C:/POLARIS/src/polaris_graph/roles/native_gate_b_inputs.py:1137) can create routed synthesized DS audit rows under `PG_SYNTH_D8_PROMOTE=1` even when `PG_DEPTH_SYNTHESIS_D8_GATE=0`, but `scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py` only runs `_depth_d8_true_drop` behind the legacy `depth_synthesis_d8_gate_enabled()` check. A promote-only synthesized finding that fails to produce a final verdict, or remains unjudged, can therefore avoid the specialized “unjudged synthesized => drop” cleanup. Default legacy-on reduces blast radius, but the promote-only OFF-path claim is not safe.

P1: The furniture strip can corrupt legitimate dated findings. [weighted_enrichment.py](C:/POLARIS/src/polaris_graph/generator/weighted_enrichment.py:3519) strips any `dd-mm-yyyy` token unconditionally across sanitized claim text. Repro: `The rule took effect on 02-10-2025 and changed reporting obligations.` becomes `The rule took effect on and changed reporting obligations.` This is not source deletion, but it is a real span-level over-strip that damages policy/legal/reporting claims.

I confirmed the important non-issues: `def strict_verify` is not in the changed hunks; C4 stable-partitions the evidence base into a trailing appendix rather than dropping it; F window snap is extend-only and bounded; I did not find a new breadth cap/target/thinner. The claimed offline suite passed locally: `89 passed`.
